        <div class="slideshow-description-container add-padding-right">
         <div class="j-desc-more description" data-ga-action="description&gt;more" data-ga-cat="bigfoot_slideview">
          <p class="notranslate">
           For years I struggled with procrastination and every year I would always look back having never met my goals. In March of 2014, I decided to figure out what I was doing wrong once and for all. And

                    
           <a href="#">
            <i class="fa fa-caret-down">
            </i>
           </a>
          </p>
         </div>
         <p class="j-desc-expand description description-expanded notranslate" itemprop="description">
          For years I struggled with procrastination and every year I would always look back having never met my goals. In March of 2014, I decided to figure out what I was doing wrong once and for all. And after 8 months of research, I finally came across the answer and it lay in habits and their powerful ability to reshape our lives.
         </p>
